Yay school's out.. but ever since school let out I have been dead
on anarchist ideas!  I guess school makes you think, sometimes not
what the teachers want you to think(like blowing up the photo 
copier, leaving the teachers stranded).  Oh well.. here's the 
lineup for this month.. oh wait a sec.  The chm's webpage is
getting a face lift, and a change of domains.. the page is
still under construction but if you'd like to check it out
its at: 
        members.tripod.com/~havoc403
Now.. here's the lineup:

This month I have been drawing a total blank!  I have no idea on what I
should write about, I guess school actually motivated my inner anarchist.
So I jumped into my backups, and this was the best one I found.  Its not
really a file, its world wide dialups to tymnet that I had buffered long
ago.  Here is the result of my computer surfing..

                    |
              \           /       By MAYHEM
               Sparkler
            -       *        -
                      Bombs
              /            \
                    |

     Ok, I'm not gonna get to descriptive because it's incredibly simple.
What you need is a metal can with a removable lid and a sparkler (preferably
the round ball kind with the fuse.  Those are the ones I'm talking about in
this text).  Well, to make this simpler, here is a list of what you need.

*STRONG* electricians tape
Metal can with lid (I'm currently experimenting with those little
                    prescription bottles that the doctor puts the pills in
                    but I'm not sure they can contain the tremendous pressure
                    this bomb makes.
Ball sparkler with fuse

     Alright, first you take the lid off the metal can and punch a hole just
big enough for the fuse to slide through.  Then tape your ball sparkler
(LOOSELY) to the underside of the lid and slide the fuse through the nice
hole that you made.  Put the lid back on and here's where your *STRONG* tape
comes in...  Tape the lid down.  Go crazy with the tape because if the lid
flies off, it can kill you.  I tape all the way around the can for a more
secure hold.
     The first time I tried this I just used some plain clear tape and after
a small "pop" the lid was embedded in a tree in my back yard.  It's still
there too.  I can't pull it out.
     Anyways, securing the lid is the most important part of this bomb.  Once
you've done everything above, you will own a deafening contraption that will
make you the most hated member of your community.  Just light the fuse, get
the hell away and cover your ears...

SUGGESTED USES
1. Slide it into your neighbor's exhaust pipe and light it...
2. Blast a mailbox
3. Put it on a doorstep in the morning.  Rise and shine....  Better not stick
   around to watch it.
4. Try adding BB gun pellets and setting it next to a car so that the seam on
   the can is facing the paint.  Uh-oh, better get Maaco...  (Untested).

FOR THE TECHNICAL PEOPLE...
     As you know, when gunpowder or any other combustable substance is lighted
it expands greatly.  That's why it only takes 20 or so grains of gunpowder to
pop a bullet out of the shell at several hundred MPH. This works on the same
concept.  As the sparkler or whatever you want to put in your SEALED
container goes off, immense pressure builds up.  So immense that if it's a
can, the seal on the side will burst and blow out some eardrums.
     As long as you don't put anything else in the can, it's completely safe
if you're far enough away.

FOR YOUR SAFETY...
1. After lighting the fuse, move at least ten yards away and cover yor ears.
2. If nothing happens and you're sure that it went off inside the can, stay
   the fuck away.  You HAD to pick NASA titanium can, didn't you.  According
   to my calculations, there are several thousand pounds of pressure in the
   can (enough to blow your hand off your arm) so find some way to puncture
   it from a distance.  If you can't, just stay away from the area for a
   while and the pressure should be released through the hole you made.  It
   might even whistle really loud...
3. After it goes off, the can will be very hot so don't mess with it for a
   minute or two... unless you LIKE 1st degree burns.

     Courtesy of ScorpioSoft and MAYHEM...  And folks remember...  If you get
hurt or into any kind of trouble, it's your own fault, not mine.

              Phun Ways To Phuck People Over

at them?  Try using these as the solution to fuck them up.  

At School:
School seems to be the best place to get them at.  Theres lots of people to 
laugh at the victim after you fuck him over.

Lockers
Best place to get someone at, all there shit is in there.  Try heating up 
his lock as much as you can before the person gets to his locker, when the 
little fuck trys to put in his combs "SSHHHH.. SHIT MY HAND!". If its a

under the number part and pop it off.  He will miss his classes because he 
cant open his locker, and he will have to cry to the school janitor to get 
it off.

Gym Class!
Now this is the best place to fuck someone over, probably the best place to

At his house.
This is the fun part, after he goes through a day of hell at school, he

His Power
Go into his backyard, find his power reader peice of shit that the electric

For Sale Signs.

                     ÚÄ Microsoft and Apple Alliance Ä¿
                     À-------------------------------ÄÙ

Microsoft is now on top!  On August 6th 1997, the director and co-founder
of Apple Computer Inc. Steve Jobs and Microsoft Corp. chairman and CEO
Bill Gates announced a broad product and technology development agreement
between Apple and Microsoft including the folowing:

          + Microsoft will develop and ship future versions of its
            popular Microsoft Office productivity suite, Internet
            Explorer and other Microsoft tools for the Mac platform.
          + Apple will bundle the Microsoft Internet Explorer browser
            with the Mac OS, making it the default browser in future
            operating system software releases.
          + The companies agreed to a broad patent cross-licensing
            agreement. It paves the way for the two companies to work
            more closely on leading-edge technologies for the Mac
            platform.
          + Apple and Microsoft plan to collaborate on technology to
            ensure compatibility between their respective Virtual
            Machines for Java and other programming languages.
          + To further support its relationship with Apple, Microsoft
            will invest $150 million in non-voting Apple stock.

Also Microsoft is investing $150 million in Apple.  Why you ask, would
Apple form any alliance?  Because Apple has lost 1.5 mil. in the last
6 months and has lost more then 3.5 mil in 2 years.  
In 1980 Apple owned 30% of the computer market, it has dropped down to 
3.2% since then.  Yes today apple only owns 3.2% of the computer market.
Face it, Mac is going down the drain and IBM is kickin ass!  "We must
let go of this notion that for Apple to win Microsoft must lose!" said
Jobs at the Macworld Expo today in Boston.  But who knows, Microsoft 
might acctually bring apple back into the scene.  Right after the 
anouncment was made Apple stocks went up by $6, and Microsoft stock
went down by $19.  Well here are a bunch of quotes from the Expo:

   "In 1984, Steve Jobs and I stood together when Microsoft announced
   Microsoft Excel, an application that is widely credited with helping
   to define the potential of the Mac as a great applications platform,"
   said Gates. "Today's announcements underscore our continued belief in
   the Mac as a platform for applications and leading -edge Internet
   technologies. Microsoft has millions of customers who rely on
   Macintosh technology and they can be assured that Microsoft products
   for the Mac will continue to be available."
   "We are thrilled at the prospect of working more closely with
   Microsoft on applications and Internet software" said Jobs. "We are
   confident that this is the beginning of a much closer relationship
   between the two companies, which will greatly benefit our common
   customers."

                  ÚÄ Hells Angels Grim Reaper patchover Ä¿
                  À-------------------------------------ÄÙ
Last month the police stormed the Grim Reaper's domain in Red Deer 
Alberta, in a desprit attempt to put their foot down on outlaw bikers, 
and crime in general.  This was also done to disscourage the large
biker gang the Hells Angels from comming and setting up a chapple here
in Alberta Canada.  
Well the police didn't do a very good job, because not only have the
Hells Angels setup a Chapple in Red Deer, Alberta.  But they have
taken over the local biker gang the Grim Reapers.  
Many Hells Angels rolled into the little town of Red Deer, which lays
in between Edmonton and Calgary(the largest cities in alberta) on monday
the 21st.  The party had already started, and 43 bikers started wearing
their hells angels colors with the lable Alberta.  Yup thats right good
old Alberta has is own chapple for the Hells Angels.  
The cops predict crime will rise cause the Angels have arrived, and
that they will be taking over most of the prostitution and drug
trafficing in Alberta.  
Some people are scared of them, some people are cautious, but most are
courious onlookers that stop by and chat with the not so welcome Hells
Angels.  All I have to say is cool.  And if there are any Hells Angels
out there that have a computer, I would love to interview you to see
what you have to say.

                      ÚÄ AOL4FREE Author tells all! Ä¿
                      À-----------------------------ÄÙ

AOL4FREE Culprit Tells His Tale
by David Cassel 
          
5:02amæ22.Apr.97.PDT Nicholas Ryan, a college junior
convicted for authoring the original AOL4FREE
program, will be leaving Yale University this June
to start a six-month home sentence, and two
years of probation. 

For 25 hours a week, he will be working at a
special education program as a form of
community service. But on off-hours, Ryan will be
working on an encryption program for Windows
95, based on the Macintosh program that stumped
the Secret Service agents who confiscated his
computer. "It would be a mini-encrypted hard
drive - every time you shut down the computer,
all the information would be totally encrypted." 

Three weeks after his conviction, Ryan says he is
ready to talk about his hacker past, and to share
his experience of creating a program in 1995 that
allowed hackers to use AOL without paying the
hourly charge. Last week, Ryan came forward with
a 30-KB essay explaining his motives and
experiences to hacker sites. His confessions
came the same week that the Department of
Energy put out a warning against the AOL4FREE
"Trojan horse," a file-destroying program that is
masquerading as Ryan's original program. 

"I was an outlaw, a spy," Ryan boasts, "and I loved
cracking the puzzle of AOL's system." During the
days of US$2.95-an-hour pricing, AOL4FREE made
Ryan, aka Happy Hardcore, a hero in hacker chat
rooms. "When I entered a room, I'd immediately
get dozens of messages asking about when my
next version would come out, who I knew, and
many just thanking me." His essay also includes
anecdotes of hacking live chats and distributing
AOL customer data. 

In a press release applauding his conviction, AOL
conceded that hundreds used the program to gain
free access to the service. Ryan's is the first
federal felony conviction involving an online
service, AOL claims. "AOL and the prosecutors
decided they wanted it to strike a blow against
the hackers and take me out as an example," Ryan
said in an interview. "At one point they were even
claiming that the damages were US$1.5 million." 

Ironically, Ryan had titled one section of the
documentation for AOL4FREE "Can I get caught?"
He even supplied a prescient answer: "A better
question would be, 'Would they want to prosecute
me if I'm caught?'" Ryan now claims he'd been
reassured by internal memos forwarded by
hacker friends that AOL would not go after him. "I
assumed they were going after the AOL4FREE
users. Kind of a dumb assumption.... The Secret
Service knocked on my door in December." 

Of the latest AOL4FREE decoy, Ryan says there's
nothing new in naming Trojan-horse programs
after real ones. "I remember during 1995, way
back then, there was an AOL4FREE program that
was actually a Trojan horse. So this program may
just be a couple of years old." 

Mixed in with the harrowing stories of his
exploits, Ryan's confessional essay includes a
disclaimer: "I stress that in no way did we EVER
do anything to cause permanent damage using the
tools or information that we found." He adds: "We
could've taken down 500 file libraries. We
could've massively wreaked havoc on the service.
But it wasn't what we were there for. It was a
puzzle of it, the challenge of it."
